update default_header set refdatacolumn_hbmname="name", validatetype="ref", dataindex="currencyName", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Currency";
update default_header set validatetype="text", dataindex="vendorInvoiceNumber", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Vendor Invoice Number";
update default_header set validatetype="date", dataindex="vendorInvoiceDate", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Vendor Invoice Date";
update default_header set refdatacolumn_hbmname="name", validatetype="ref", dataindex="costcenter", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Cost Center";
update default_header set dataindex="shipdate", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Ship Date";
update default_header set pojomethodname="Termid", refmodule_pojoclassname="Term", refdatacolumn_hbmname="termname", reffetchcolumn_hbmname="ID", validatetype="ref", dataindex="term", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Term";
update default_header set dataindex="dueDate", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Due Date";
update default_header set ismandatory = 'F', hbmnotnull = 'F', validatetype="text", dataindex="memo", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Memo";
update default_header set ismandatory = 'F', hbmnotnull = 'F', dataindex="shipvia", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Ship via";
update default_header set ismandatory = 'F', hbmnotnull = 'F', dataindex="fob", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "FOB";
update default_header set refmodule_pojoclassname="MasterItem", refdatacolumn_hbmname="value", reffetchcolumn_hbmname="ID", validatetype="ref", dataindex="agent", isdocumentimport = 'T', allowimport=1 where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Agent";
update default_header set pojomethodname="GoodsReceiptNo", validatetype="text", dataindex="goodsReceiptNo", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Goods Receipt No";
update default_header set pojomethodname="Discount", validatetype="double", dataindex="discount", isdocumentimport = 'T' where module=6 and defaultHeader = "Discount";

# Suhas Chaware 6 June 2016

    CREATE TABLE `labour_skill_mapping` (
`id`  varchar(255) NOT NULL ,
`labour`  varchar(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL ,
`skill`  varchar(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
`company`  varchar(255) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`labour`) REFERENCES `labour` (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`skill`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`))
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8;

INSERT INTO labour_skill_mapping (id, labour,skill,company)
(SELECT UUID(),id,keyskill,company FROM labour GROUP BY id);

ALTER TABLE labour DROP FOREIGN KEY `FK_labour_skill`;
alter table labour drop column keyskill;
ALTER TABLE labour MODIFY dob date NULL DEFAULT NULL;
ALTER TABLE labour MODIFY nationality  varchar(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL;
ALTER TABLE labour MODIFY countryorigin varchar(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL;
ALTER TABLE labour MODIFY residentstatus varchar(50) NULL DEFAULT NULL;
ALTER TABLE labour MODIFY religion varchar(50) NULL DEFAULT NULL;
ALTER TABLE labour MODIFY race varchar(50) NULL DEFAULT NULL;

update reportmaster set name = "Custom Column Line Detail Report" where name="Custom column Line Detail Report";

CREATE TABLE `widgetreportmaster` (
`id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
`report` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
`company` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
KEY `fk_widgetreportmaster_report` (`report`),
KEY `fk_widgetreportmaster_company` (`company`),
CONSTRAINT `fk_widgetreportmaster_company` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
CONSTRAINT `fk_widgetreportmaster_report` FOREIGN KEY (`report`) REFERENCES `reportmaster` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

alter table reportmaster add column widgetURL text;
alter table reportmaster add column isWidgetReady char(1) DEFAULT 'F';

update reportmaster set widgetURL="ACCInvoiceCMN/getDailySalesReport.do?isWidgetRequest=true&mode=18&creditonly=false&nondeleted=true&getRepeateInvoice=false&consolidateFlag=$consolidateFlag$&companyids=$companyids$&gcurrencyid=$gcurrencyid$&loginid=$loginid$&stdate=$stdate$&enddate=$enddate$", isWidgetReady='T' where id="Daily_Sales_Report";

CREATE TABLE `excisedetailsassets` (
`id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`quotation` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
`purchaseorder` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
`supplier` varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
`suppliertinsalestaxno` varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
`supplierexciseregnno` varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
`cstnumber` varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
`supplierrange` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`suppliercommissionerate` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`supplieraddress` varchar(1024)  DEFAULT "",
`supplierstate` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`supplierimporterexportercode` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`supplierdivision` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturername` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturerexciseregnno` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturerrange` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturercommissionerate` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturerdivision` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufactureraddress` varchar(1024)  DEFAULT "",
`manufacturerimporterexportercode` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufactureinvoiceno` varchar(255)  DEFAULT "",
`manufactureinvoicedate` date DEFAULT NULL, 
PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`quotation`) REFERENCES `vendorquotation` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
FOREIGN KEY (`purchaseorder`) REFERENCES `purchaseorder` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
)
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

ALTER TABLE exciseInvoicedetails DROP FOREIGN KEY exciseInvoicedetails_ibfk_2;
ALTER TABLE exciseInvoicedetails DROP COLUMN supplierstate;
ALTER TABLE exciseInvoicedetails ADD COLUMN supplierstate VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT"";

CREATE TABLE `customreportsmeasuresfields` (
  `measurefieldid` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  `measurefieldname` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `measurefielddisplayname` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `createdon` BIGINT(25) NULL,
  `updatedon` BIGINT(25) NULL,
  `createdbyid` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `updatedbyid` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `xtype` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `measurefieldmodulecategory` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `measurefieldmodule` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`measurefieldid`),
  KEY `fk_customreportsmeasuresfields_1_idx` (`createdbyid`),
  KEY `updatedbyid` (`updatedbyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreportsmeasuresfields_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`createdbyid`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreportsmeasuresfields_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`updatedbyid`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreportsmeasuresfields_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`measurefieldmodulecategory`) REFERENCES `moduleCategory` (`moduleCatId`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreportsmeasuresfields_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`measurefieldmodule`) REFERENCES `modules` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


CREATE TABLE `customreportsmeasuresfieldsmapping` (
  `id` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  `measurefieldid` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `defaultheaderid` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreportsmeasuresfieldsmapping_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`measurefieldid`) REFERENCES `customreportsmeasuresfields` (`measurefieldid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Vipin Gupta 20th June 2016
ALTER TABLE `olympus_importscriptinfo`
DROP PRIMARY KEY;
ALTER TABLE `olympus_importscriptinfo`
ADD COLUMN `recid`  bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT FIRST ,
ADD PRIMARY KEY (`recid`);

CREATE TABLE `olympus_import_filepath` (
`recid`  bigint NOT NULL ,
`filepath`  varchar(255) NOT NULL ,
PRIMARY KEY (`recid`, `filepath`),
FOREIGN KEY (`recid`) REFERENCES `olympus_importscriptinfo` (`recid`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
)
ENGINE=InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_general_ci
;

#Akshay Gujar 20th June 2016
ALTER TABLE invoicedetailtermsmap ADD COLUMN `creditavailedflag` int(1) DEFAULT '0';
ALTER TABLE receiptdetailtermsmap ADD COLUMN `creditavailedflag` int(1) DEFAULT '0';

update invoicedetailtermsmap inner join linelevelterms on invoicedetailtermsmap.term=linelevelterms.id set creditavailedflag = 1, taxpaidflag = 0 where taxpaidflag = 1 and linelevelterms.termtype=2;
update receiptdetailtermsmap inner join linelevelterms on receiptdetailtermsmap.term=linelevelterms.id set creditavailedflag = 1, taxpaidflag = 0 where taxpaidflag = 1 and linelevelterms.termtype=2;

CREATE TABLE `journalentryupdatehistory` (
`id`  varchar(255) NOT NULL ,
`jeid`  varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL ,
`jedid`  varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`transactionid`  varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`transactionmoduleid` int(11) DEFAULT 0,
`oldamountinbase` double DEFAULT 0,
`newamountinbase` double DEFAULT 0,
`oldamount` double DEFAULT 0,
`newamount` double DEFAULT 0,
`exchangerate` double DEFAULT 0,
`company`  varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`updatedate` date DEFAULT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`))
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8;

#Mohammed Uzair Momin 23rd June 2016
CREATE TABLE `disposerevertassets` (
  `id` VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  `asset` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `company` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `disposalJE` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reverseJE` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `isreverted` int(1) DEFAULT '0',
  
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `FK_disposerevertassets_asset` (`asset`),
  KEY `FK_disposerevertassets_company` (`company`),
  KEY `FK_disposerevertassets_disposalJE` (`disposalJE`),
  KEY `FK_disposerevertassets_reverseJE` (`reverseJE`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_disposerevertassets_asset` FOREIGN KEY (`asset`) REFERENCES `assetdetail` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_disposerevertassets_company` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_disposerevertassets_disposalJE` FOREIGN KEY (`disposalJE`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_disposerevertassets_reverseJE` FOREIGN KEY (`reverseJE`) REFERENCES `journalentry` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

ALTER TABLE purchaseorder ADD COLUMN isexpensetype CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'F';	

CREATE TABLE expensepodetails (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `srno` int(3) DEFAULT '0',
  `rate` double NOT NULL,
  `amount` double NOT NULL,
  `rowtaxamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `description` text,
  `rateIncludingGst` double DEFAULT '0',
  `isdebit` char(1) DEFAULT 'T',
  `tax` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `account` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `discount` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `purchaseorder` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `expensepodetails_FK_1` FOREIGN KEY (`account`) REFERENCES `account` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `expensepodetails_FK_2` FOREIGN KEY (`tax`) REFERENCES `tax` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `expensepodetails_FK_3` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `expensepodetails_FK_4` FOREIGN KEY (`discount`) REFERENCES `discount` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `expensepodetails_FK_5` FOREIGN KEY (`purchaseorder`) REFERENCES `purchaseorder` (`id`)
)ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8;

ALTER TABLE moduleCategory RENAME modulecategory;
ALTER TABLE modulecategory CHANGE moduleCatId modulecatid VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL;
ALTER TABLE modulecategory CHANGE moduleCatname modulecatname VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL;
ALTER TABLE customreports DROP FOREIGN KEY `customreports_ibfk_3`;
ALTER TABLE `customreports` ADD CONSTRAINT `customreports_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`reportmodulecategory`) REFERENCES `modulecategory` (`modulecatid`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION;

ALTER TABLE customreportsdefaultfieldsmapping CHANGE isSelectDataIndex isselectdataindex boolean NULL default false;
ALTER TABLE default_header CHANGE isDefaultFieldMappings isdefaultfieldmappings boolean NULL default false;
ALTER TABLE default_header CHANGE isDataIndex isdataindex boolean NULL default true;

DROP TABLE customreportsmeasuresfieldsmapping;
DROP TABLE customreportsmeasuresfields;

CREATE TABLE `customreportsmeasuresfields` (
  `measurefieldid` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  `measurefieldname` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `measurefielddisplayname` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `createdon` BIGINT(25) NULL,
  `updatedon` BIGINT(25) NULL,
  `xtype` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `measurefieldmodulecategory` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `measurefieldmodule` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`measurefieldid`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreportsmeasuresfields_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`measurefieldmodulecategory`) REFERENCES `modulecategory` (`modulecatid`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreportsmeasuresfields_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`measurefieldmodule`) REFERENCES `modules` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


CREATE TABLE `customreportsmeasuresfieldsmapping` (
  `id` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  `measurefieldid` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `defaultheaderid` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `isdataindex` boolean NULL default false,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreportsmeasuresfieldsmapping_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`measurefieldid`) REFERENCES `customreportsmeasuresfields` (`measurefieldid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
